9th-32nd Decklists
==================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 13, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











In addition to the [Top 8 decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpsao17/top-8-decklists-2017-08-13), we were able to translate and produce the Top 32 decklists with some extra helping hands. However, a catastrophe hit us sometime in the evening, when we were attacked by a flock of rabid sheep who decided the deck check area was a paper buffet. Well, long story short, we’re a couple short. Excluding Fernando Gonzalez’s 18th place decklist and Charlie Vieira’s 32nd place decklists (good job too, you guys!), the rest of these 22 decklists should provide a clear indication of the top performing decks of the weekend!


The metagame was packed with Grixis Shadow and Titan Shift, but some interesting decks such as Faeries, Skred Red, Jeskai Midrange (oooh... Lightning Angel!), Gifts Storm, Naya Titan Breach, and Gifts Storm also made their way to the top of the pack!







#### Guilherme Lundgren's Grixis Shadow


##### 
 Grand Prix São Paulo 2017 – 9th






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
